GT*(c1*epsilon+c2) = (4.2784*T*epsilon**3 - 0.2857*T + 28.5804*epsilon**2 - 1205.86*epsilon**3 + 80.537)*(c1*epsilon+c2)

This would produce terms like `T*epsilon**4`, `T*epsilon**3`, `T*epsilon`, `T`, `epsilon**3`, `epsilon**2`, `epsilon**4`, `epsilon`, constant, `epsilon**5`, etc.

The numerator of candidate 6 has T terms from `T*c3*(c4+epsilon)**3 + T*c5*epsilon*(c4+epsilon)**3`:
With c4=0: `T*c3*epsilon**3 + T*c5*epsilon**4` → can produce `T*epsilon**3` and `T*epsilon**4`. ✓
Plus `T*c0` → `T` term. ✓

Non-T terms: `c1*epsilon**3 + (c2+c7)*epsilon**2 + (c8+c9)*epsilon + c6`
But GT*(c1*epsilon+c2) would need `epsilon**4` and `epsilon**5` terms from the non-T part. The numerator doesn't have those. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 7:** Similar rational structure. Same issue. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 44, 45:** Similar rational structures. Let me check 44.
All terms divided by `(c1*epsilon+c2)`. Numerator: `T*c0 + c1*epsilon**3 + c2*epsilon**2 + c3 + c4*epsilon**5 + c5*epsilon**2 + c6*epsilon + c7*epsilon**4 + c8*epsilon`

For this to equal GT, numerator = GT*(c1*epsilon+c2).
GT*(c1*epsilon+c2) has T*epsilon**4, T*epsilon**3, T*epsilon, T terms. But numerator only has T*c0 (linear in T, no epsilon). Can't produce T*epsilon**3. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 45:** Same as 44 with extra constant. Same issue. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 41:** Has exp terms. Complex. The T dependence is only through `T*c0/(c1*epsilon+c2)`. Can't produce `T*epsilon**3`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 50:** `T*c0/(c1*epsilon+c2) + T**c3*c4 + c5*exp(c6*epsilon) + c7*epsilon**c8 + c9/(c1*epsilon+c2)`
Has `T**c3` which with c3=1 gives T. And `T*c0/(c1*epsilon+c2)` - if c1=0, this gives T*c0/c2 (another T term). But then no `T*epsilon**3`. If c1≠0, `T*c0/(c1*epsilon+c2)` can't produce `T*epsilon**3`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 24:** `T*c0/(T*c1+c2) + T*c3*(c4+epsilon)**c5 + c6*epsilon**2 + c7*epsilon + c8 + c9/(T*c1+c2)`
`T*c0/(T*c1+c2)` - if c1=0: `T*c0/c2` = constant*T. 
`T*c3*(c4+epsilon)**c5` with c4=0, c5=3: `T*c3*epsilon**3`. ✓
So: `a*T + T*c3*epsilon**3 + c6*epsilon**2 + c7*epsilon + c8 + c9/c2`
= `T*c3*epsilon**3 + a*T + c6*epsilon**2 + c7*epsilon + (c8+c9/c2)`
Missing `epsilon**3`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 3:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + T**c2*c3 + c4*epsilon**2 + c5 + c6*sin(c7*epsilon+c8)`
With c1=0: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + T**c2*c3 + c4*epsilon**2 + c5 + c6*sin(...)`
Set c2=1: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + c3*T + c4*epsilon**2 + c5 + c6*sin(...)`
Missing `epsilon**3`. sin can't produce `epsilon**3` for all epsilon. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 1:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + T*c2*(c3+epsilon)**2 + c4*epsilon**2 + c5 + c6*sin(c7*epsilon+c8)`
With c1=0: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + T*c2*(c3+epsilon)**2 + c4*epsilon**2 + c5 + c6*sin(...)`
Expand `T*c2*(c3+epsilon)**2` = `T*c2*c3**2 + 2*T*c2*c3*epsilon + T*c2*epsilon**2`
GT has no `T*epsilon` or `T*epsilon**2`, so `2*c2*c3 = 0` and `c2 = 0`.
If c2=0: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + c4*epsilon**2 + c5 + c6*sin(...)`. Missing `T`, `epsilon**3`. **NO MATCH**
If c3=0: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + T*c2*epsilon**2 + c4*epsilon**2 + c5 + c6*sin(...)`. Has unwanted `T*epsilon**2`. Must set c2=0. Same result. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 12:** `T*c0 + c1*epsilon**2 + c2*epsilon**4 + c3*log(T*c4+1) + c5*epsilon + c6 + c7*sin(c8*epsilon+c9)`
Has log(T*c4+1) which is not linear in T. Can't produce `T*epsilon**3`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 13:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + T + c2 + c3*log(T*c4+1) + c5*epsilon**2 + c6*epsilon + c7*epsilon + c8*epsilon`
With c1=0: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + T + c3*log(T*c4+1) + c5*epsilon**2 + (c6+c7+c8)*epsilon + c2`
Has log(T*c4+1). If c3=0: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + T + c5*epsilon**2 + ...epsilon + c2`. Missing `epsilon**3`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 14:** Similar with log. Same issue. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 15:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + T + c2*epsilon**2 + c3*epsilon + c4*epsilon/(T*c5+c6) + c7/(T*c5+c6) + c8*epsilon + c9`
With c1=0: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + T + c2*epsilon**2 + (c3+c8)*epsilon + c4*epsilon/(T*c5+c6) + c7/(T*c5+c6) + c9`
The rational terms in T can't produce `epsilon**3`. If c5=0: `c4*epsilon/c6 + c7/c6` are constants. Then: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + T + c2*epsilon**2 + ...epsilon + constant`. Missing `epsilon**3`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 16:** `T*c0 + c1*epsilon**2 + c2*epsilon**4 + c3*exp(T*c4) + c5*epsilon + c6 + c7*sin(c8*epsilon+c9)`
Has exp(T*c4). If c4=0: c3*1 = constant. Then `T*c0 + c1*epsilon**2 + c2*epsilon**4 + c5*epsilon + (c6+c3) + c7*sin(...)`. Missing `T*epsilon**3`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 17-18:** Similar. Missing `T*epsilon**3`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 20:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + T + T**c2*c3 + c4*epsilon**2 + c5*epsilon + c6*epsilon + c7`
With c1=0: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + T + T**c2*c3 + c4*epsilon**2 + (c5+c6)*epsilon + c7`
Set c2=1: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + T*(1+c3) + c4*epsilon**2 + (c5+c6)*epsilon + c7`
Missing `epsilon**3`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 22:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + T + T**c2*c3 + c4 + c5*epsilon**2 + c6*epsilon + c7*epsilon + c8*epsilon`
Same as 20 essentially. Missing `epsilon**3`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 23:** `T*c0 + c1*epsilon**2 + c2*epsilon**c3 + c4*epsilon + c5 + c6*sin(c7*epsilon+c8)`
Has `T*c0` but no `T*epsilon**3`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 29:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + c2*epsilon**2 + c3*sin(c4*epsilon+c5)`
With c1=0: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + c2*epsilon**2 + c3*sin(...)`. Missing `T`, `epsilon**3`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 30:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + c2 + c3*sin(c4*epsilon+c5)`
With c1=0: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + c2 + c3*sin(...)`. Missing `T`, `epsilon**2`, `epsilon**3`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 31:** `T*c0 + T**c1*c2 + c3*epsilon**2 + c4*epsilon**4 + c5*epsilon + c6 + c7*sin(c8*epsilon+c9)`
No `T*epsilon**3`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 32-39:** All have `T*c0` linear, no `T*epsilon**3`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 43:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + c2*epsilon**2 + c3*exp(c4*epsilon) + c5 + c6*sin(c7*epsilon+c8)`
With c1=0: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + c2*epsilon**2 + c3*exp(c4*epsilon) + c5 + c6*sin(...)`. Missing `T`. exp and sin can't produce `T`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 49:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + c2 + c3*sin(c4*epsilon+c5) + epsilon**2`
With c1=0: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + epsilon**2 + c2 + c3*sin(...)`. Missing `T`, `epsilon**3`. **NO MATCH**

Let me reconsider candidates more carefully. The GT needs: `T*epsilon**3`, `T`, `epsilon**2`, `epsilon**3`, constant.

Looking back at **Candidate 8**: `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + T*c2 + T*c3*epsilon + T + c4 + c5*epsilon**2 + c6*epsilon + c7*epsilon + c8*epsilon`

What if c1≠0? Then we get `T*c0*(c1^3 + 3c1^2*epsilon + 3c1*epsilon^2 + epsilon^3) + T*c2 + T*c3*epsilon + T + c4 + c5*epsilon^2 + (c6+c7+c8)*epsilon`

T-dependent: `T*(c0*c1^3 + c2 + 1) + T*(3c0*c1^2 + c3)*epsilon + T*3c0*c1*epsilon^2 + T*c0*epsilon^3`

For GT: T*epsilon^3 coefficient = 4.2784 → c0 = 4.2784
T*epsilon^2 coefficient = 0 → 3*c0*c1 = 0 → c1 = 0
Then T*epsilon coefficient = c3 → must be 0
T constant = c0*0 + c2 + 1 = c2 + 1 → need c2+1 = -0.2857 → c2 = -1.2857

Non-T: c4 + c5*epsilon^2 + (c6+c7+c8)*epsilon
Need: 28.5804*epsilon^2 - 1205.86*epsilon^3 + 80.537

Missing `epsilon**3`! **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 9:** Same analysis. Missing `epsilon**3`. **NO MATCH**

Hmm, none of the candidates seem to have both `T*epsilon**3` and standalone `epsilon**3` unless they use a different mechanism.

Wait, let me re-examine **Candidate 10**: `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + T*c2*(c3+epsilon)**c4 + T + c5 + c6*epsilon**2 + c7*epsilon + c8*epsilon + c9*epsilon`

With c1=0: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + T*c2*(c3+epsilon)**c4 + T + c5 + c6*epsilon**2 + (c7+c8+c9)*epsilon`

What if c4=3, c3≠0? `T*c2*(c3+epsilon)**3 = T*c2*(c3^3 + 3c3^2*epsilon + 3c3*epsilon^2 + epsilon^3)`

Total T-dependent: `T*(c0+c2)*epsilon^3 + T*3c2*c3*epsilon^2 + T*3c2*c3^2*epsilon + T*(c2*c3^3+1)`

Need: T*epsilon^3 coeff = 4.2784, T*epsilon^2 coeff = 0, T*epsilon coeff = 0, T coeff = -0.2857

From T*epsilon^2: 3c2*c3 = 0. If c3=0: same as before, c2 just adds to c0. T coeff = 1 → need -0.2857, impossible unless... wait, T coeff = c2*0 + 1 = 1. We need -0.2857. Can't match. If c2=0: T*c0*epsilon^3 + T. T coeff = 1 ≠ -0.2857. **NO MATCH**

Actually wait - what about setting c4 to a non-integer? If c4=0: `T*c2*1 = T*c2`. Then T terms: `T*c0*epsilon^3 + T*c2 + T = T*c0*epsilon^3 + T*(c2+1)`. Set c2+1 = -0.2857. Non-T: `c5 + c6*epsilon^2 + (c7+c8+c9)*epsilon`. Missing `epsilon**3`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 11:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + T*c2*(c3+epsilon)**c4 + T + c5*epsilon**2 + c6*epsilon + c7*epsilon + c8`
Same analysis. With c1=0, c4=0: `T*c0*epsilon^3 + T*(c2+1) + c5*epsilon^2 + (c6+c7)*epsilon + c8`. Missing `epsilon**3`. **NO MATCH**

Now I'm starting to think none match. But let me be more careful about some candidates.

**Candidate 6 revisited:** All terms over `(c1*epsilon+c2)`.

Numerator = `T*c0 + T*c3*(c4+epsilon)^3 + T*c5*epsilon*(c4+epsilon)^3 + c1*epsilon^3 + c2*epsilon^2 + c6 + c7*epsilon^2 + c8*epsilon + c9*epsilon`

For this to equal GT*(c1*epsilon+c2):

GT*(c1*epsilon+c2) = [4.2784*T*epsilon^3 - 0.2857*T + 28.5804*epsilon^2 - 1205.86*epsilon^3 + 80.537]*(c1*epsilon+c2)

= c1*4.2784*T*epsilon^4 + c2*4.2784*T*epsilon^3 - c1*0.2857*T*epsilon - c2*0.2857*T + c1*28.5804*epsilon^3 - c1*1205.86*epsilon^4 + c2*28.5804*epsilon^2 - c2*1205.86*epsilon^3 + c1*80.537*epsilon + c2*80.537

T-dependent terms in numerator:
`T*c0 + T*c3*(c4+epsilon)^3 + T*c5*epsilon*(c4+epsilon)^3`

With c4=0:
`T*c0 + T*c3*epsilon^3 + T*c5*epsilon^4`

Matching T terms:
- T*epsilon^4: c5 = c1*4.2784
- T*epsilon^3: c3 = c2*4.2784
- T*epsilon: 0 = -c1*0.2857 → c1 = 0
- T: c0 = -c2*0.2857

If c1=0: c5=0, and denominator = c2 (constant).

Then numerator non-T: `0 + c2*epsilon^2 + c6 + c7*epsilon^2 + c8*epsilon + c9*epsilon`
= `(c2+c7)*epsilon^2 + (c8+c9)*epsilon + c6`

GT*c2 non-T: `c2*28.5804*epsilon^2 - c2*1205.86*epsilon^3 + c2*80.537`

Need epsilon^3 term: -c2*1205.86*epsilon^3. But numerator has no epsilon^3 term (c1=0 means c1*epsilon^3 = 0). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 7:** Similar. With c1=0, denominator=c2. 
Numerator T-terms: `T*c0 + T*c3*epsilon*(c4+epsilon)^3`
With c4=0: `T*c0 + T*c3*epsilon^4`. Has T*epsilon^4 but no T*epsilon^3. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 44:** Numerator: `T*c0 + c1*epsilon^3 + c2*epsilon^2 + c3 + c4*epsilon^5 + c5*epsilon^2 + c6*epsilon + c7*epsilon^4 + c8*epsilon`
Only T term is T*c0. For GT*(c1*epsilon+c2) we need T*epsilon^4 and T*epsilon^3 terms. Can't produce them. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 45:** Same as 44 with extra constant. **NO MATCH**

Let me look at remaining candidates I haven't fully analyzed:

**Candidate 33-39:** All `T*c0 + ...` without `T*epsilon^3`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 51-54:** All `T*c0 + ...`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 47:** `T*c0 + T*c1 + c2*epsilon^2 + c3 + c4*epsilon^4 + c5*epsilon + c6*sin(c7*epsilon+c8)`
= `T*(c0+c1) + ...`. No `T*epsilon^3`. **NO MATCH**

I've now checked all 54 candidates. None of them can produce the required combination of `T*epsilon**3`, `T`, `epsilon**2`, `epsilon**3`, and constant that the GT requires.

Wait, let me double-check a few more carefully.

**Candidate 25:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + c2*epsilon**2 + c3*epsilon + c4*epsilon + c5`

What if we DON'T set c1=0? We get:
T terms: `T*c0*c1^3 + 3T*c0*c1^2*epsilon + 3T*c0*c1*epsilon^2 + T*c0*epsilon^3`
Non-T: `c2*epsilon^2 + (c3+c4)*epsilon + c5`

GT: `4.2784*T*epsilon^3 + (-0.2857)*T + 28.5804*epsilon^2 + (-1205.86)*epsilon^3 + 80.537`

From T*epsilon^3: c0 = 4.2784
From T*epsilon^2: 3*c0*c1 = 0 → c1 = 0
From T*epsilon: 0 (satisfied)
From T: c0*c1^3 = -0.2857 → 0 = -0.2857. **Contradiction!**

So c1=0 forces the T coefficient to be 0, but GT needs -0.2857. This is the fundamental issue with all `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)^3` candidates that don't have a separate `T` term.

Candidates that DO have a separate T term (like `+T` or `+T*c2`):

**Candidate 8, 9, 10, 11, 19, 20, 21, 22** all have `+T` or `+T*c2`. With c1=0 in the cubic, they provide `T*c0*epsilon^3 + T*(something)`. The T coefficient can be adjusted. But they're all missing `epsilon^3`.

Unless... can any of these produce `epsilon^3` through some mechanism?

**Candidate 10:** Has `T*c2*(c3+epsilon)**c4`. If c4 is not an integer... but this always has T multiplied. Can't produce standalone `epsilon^3`.

**Candidate 11:** Same issue.

**Candidate 20, 22:** Have `T**c2*c3`. If c2=0: `c3*1 = c3` (constant). Can't produce `epsilon^3`.

Hmm. What about candidates with sin terms? Could `sin(c*epsilon)` approximate `epsilon^3`? No - sin is a different basis function. Strict algebraic equivalence is required.

What about candidates with `epsilon**c` where c is free?

**Candidate 2:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**3 + c2*epsilon**c3 + c4*epsilon**2 + c5 + c6*sin(c7*epsilon+c8)`
With c1=0: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + c2*epsilon**c3 + c4*epsilon**2 + c5 + c6*sin(...)`
Set c3=3: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + c2*epsilon**3 + c4*epsilon**2 + c5 + c6*sin(...)`
Missing `T` term. sin can't produce T. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 23:** `T*c0 + c1*epsilon**2 + c2*epsilon**c3 + c4*epsilon + c5 + c6*sin(c7*epsilon+c8)`
No `T*epsilon**3`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 26:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)**c2 + c3*epsilon**2 + c4*epsilon + c5`
With c1=0, c2=3: `T*c0*epsilon**3 + c3*epsilon**2 + c4*epsilon + c5`. Missing T, epsilon^3. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 38, 39:** Have `c2*epsilon**c3` but also `T*c0` only. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 50:** `T*c0/(T*c1+c2) + T**c3*c4 + c5*exp(c6*epsilon) + c7*epsilon**c8 + c9/(T*c1+c2)`
If c1=0: `T*c0/c2 + T**c3*c4 + c5*exp(c6*epsilon) + c7*epsilon**c8 + c9/c2`
Set c3=1: `T*(c0/c2+c4) + c5*exp(c6*epsilon) + c7*epsilon**c8 + (c9/c2)`
No `T*epsilon**3`. 
What if c3=4? `T**4*c4` - wrong.
What about c1≠0? `T*c0/(T*c1+c2)` is a nonlinear function of T. Can't produce `T*epsilon**3`. **NO MATCH**

I've exhaustively checked all candidates. None can produce the required set of basis functions {T*epsilon^3, T, epsilon^2, epsilon^3, constant} that the GT demands.
